### Beauveria bassiana (Balsamo)
‡πÅ‡∏°‡∏•‡∏á ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢ (‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏ß)

## [Coffee & Tea Forum](https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/1drkK2Qz622n3Ul6RpK4e8Ve5A9Qb0F-P)

### Tea Industry in China
The development of modern tea industry in China
- Largest tea production and tea consumption (90% are consumed in-country)
- Yunnan, Fujian, Hubei is the top producers
- Traditional tea production : Green tea, Dark tea, Black tea, White tea, Yellow tea
	- Processing methods affects flavors
- International influence
	- May 21 : UN International Tea Day
Technology Innovation on tea industry in China
- Genetics and Breeding
	- Gene Chips
- Tea Garden Management
- Tea Leaves Harvest
- Tea Quality Control
- Tea Processing
- Nutrition and Health
Challenge and Opportunity of Tea Industry
### Thai Tea
Tea & Tomorrow: Building a Sustainable Thai Tea Industry with Singha Park Chiang Rai
From Farm to Factory
- Maruzen Tea Japan : Japanese Tea Matcha, Sencha, Hojicha
- NORTE
Singha Park Chaing Rai Capability
International Accreditation
### Australian Tea
Australian Tea Market Overview
- Strong coffee culture while tea and non alcohol beverage demand is rising
- Import from India and Sri Lanka
- Tea production
- Australian Tea Masters
- Market Demand
	- High Quality and Exotic origin
	- Wellness: zero alcohol, zero sugar (SINENSIS)
	- Ready To Drink and Clod Brew
	- Blending: Native natural extract blend with tea
	- Matcha with many varieties
		- Mushroom with Matcha for Umami savory
Other Tea Market
- China
- Indonesia
- Singapore
- Japan
- South Korea
- USA
- Taiwan: Tea and Fashion
- India: Premium Tea and Package
- Vietnam
Global Drivers
### Japanese Tea
Japanese Tea Industry
- Tea Cultivation area and production is decreasing due to decline of farmer
- Average Tea price (Shizuoka Tea Market) is falling since 2010 due to decline in high quality tea demand
- Green Tea Consumption is decreased by 20% while imports is decreased by 80%
- Annual expenditure on green tea and tea beverages per household is increasing but shift from tea leaves to tea beverages
- Green tea export is increasing
Word Green Tea Association 
- Collecting and disseminating information about tea from around the world
### Europe
- Matcha popularity continue in both dessert and beverage
- Native botanical
- Tea with Low carbon footprint: where and how the tea grown?
- Tea and food pairing: Alchemist, Copenhagen
- Values over volume: natural, traceable, functional health, terroir, aesthetic simplicity
### Indonesia Tea
### Thailand Coffee
Doi Tung Development Project : Coffee instead of Opium
- Supporting and Scaling
	- Chiang Rai
	- Nan
	- Myanmar
- Traceability
- Research and Development
	- Coffee Varieties in Thailand: Bourbon, Caturra, Catimor, Castillo, Paraiso, Typica, Geisha, Pacamara, Java, Gayo
	- Soil
- Quality Control
### Singapore Coffee
The 2035 Coffee Map
- Climate-proof
- Data-Driven Differentials
	- Flavour forecasting
- Pricing under pressure
	- human rights: fair wages
	- pop-up economy
	- zero-waste
	- coffee culture tourism
	- hyper personalized subscription
### Indonesia Coffee
Indonesia
- 18k Islands: Tropical, Tropical Monsoon, Tropical Savanna and Highland Climate
	- Location-specific coffee cultivation technologies
- Total Coffee Planation : 1.2 hectares, 
	- 99% smallholders (0.5-2 ha)
		- Potential for a diverse, decentralized coffee ecosystem
		- Community driven
	- Low productivity
		- Organic by default
	- Limited Infrastructure
Indonesian Coffee and cocoa research institute (ICCR)
- Global Challenges
	- Global warming

- Agroforestry coffee 
### Myanmar Coffee
Myanmar Coffee Market
- Annual production: 7000-9000 tons
- Growing regions: Shan, Mandalay, Chin, Kayin, Tanintharyi, Ayarwaddy, Magwe, Bago
- 70% exported to Japan, USA, EU, China, Thailand
- Emerging local specialty market
Myanmar Coffee Association Role
- Capacity building: Training and certification, Myanmar Coffee Institute
- Quality improvement: Competitions, processing techniques
- Market development: Trade shows, branding, IP rights, GI
- Sustainability: Agroforestry, organic practices
- Policy advocacy: Export, finances

### Vietnam Coffee
- Sustainable Development
- 4000+ Tracable coffee farmers
- Specialty coffee development in robusta

	- ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏≥
	- ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏Å

	- ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≥ ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡πÜ ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö

### ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ù‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥
‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ú‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏î ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏á

574 - ‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏ô 3 + ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡πá‡∏° 2
834 - ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏ß 1 + ‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏ô 1

> ‡πÇ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≤ ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏Ñ ‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏ü‡∏£‡∏™‡πÇ‡∏ã‡πà  ‡∏ö‡∏î‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ö ‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î 5 ‡∏ß‡∏¥

### ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ù‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏î 
‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏° ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ü‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏î
Citric ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏° ‡∏°‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
Malic ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏• ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ü‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏î‡∏µ
Tartaric ‡∏°‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏° ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ù‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÜ ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
Lactic ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏µ‡πâ ‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏±‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏î‡∏∑‡πà‡∏° ‡∏ô‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÜ

> ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Å ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà pH ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Brix ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤

### Cupping
‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏±‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏Å‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ü ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏¥‡πà‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πá‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö - Ted Lingle 2001

> ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ü‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏™‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Cupping ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ü‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏Å ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°‡πâ ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏° Cupping

### ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ù‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Cupping
‡∏Å‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ü‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á
- Fragrance 7.25 EN/SB
- Aroma 7.25
- Flavor - dry at cold
- Aftertaste - med-long nutty chocolate
- Acidity - low malic acid
- Body - juicy, little astringency 
- Balance - well balance
- Score - 81-83

## Advance Cupping & Sensory Skills Course
### Sensory Analysis ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏±‡∏™
